\xe2\x80\x93 a new series from our kitchens to yours. From our Chick-fil-A family to yours, let\xe2\x80\x99s come together around this delicious recipe from one member of our Field Operations team, Mandy Dawkins and her kids Wyatt and Conoly \xe2\x80\x93 Chick-fil-A Chicken Tetrazzini! \\nIngredients:\\r\\n1 12 count Chick-fil-A Grilled or Original Nuggets, chopped\\r\\n\xc2\xbd package spaghetti noodles\\r\\n\xc2\xbc cup butter\\r\\n1 medium onion, diced\\r\\n1 tsp minced garlic\\r\\n1 tsp dried basil\\r\\n4-7 oz canned mushroom slices (depending on how much you like mushrooms) \\n1 cup shredded cheddar cheese\\r\\n1 cup shredded Monterey jack cheese\\r\\n1 cup sour cream\\r\\n1\\/3 cup milk\\r\\n\xc2\xbd cup Parmesan cheese \\nDirections:\\r\\nWash hands for 20 seconds using soap and warm water. For best quality, use chicken immediately \\nafter purchase. If not using chicken immediately, pop in the fridge as soon as possible after purchase and remove once ready for prep. \\n1. Preheat oven to 350. \\n2. In a large pot of boiling water, cook spaghetti noodles and set aside. \\n3. In a medium saucepan, saut\xc3\xa9 onions in butter. Add garlic, dried basil and Chick-fil-A Chicken \\nNuggets. Cook over medium heat until chicken is heated through.\\r\\n4. Mix all remaining ingredients except the Parmesan cheese. \\n5. Place in greased 13x9 casserole dish and top with Parmesan cheese. Bake for 30-45 minutes (or \\nuntil bubbly and cheese is melted). Nuggets \xe2\x80\x93 a new series from our kitchens to yours. While you\xe2\x80\x99re at home, we thought we\xe2\x80\x99d share some creative ways to change up your dinner routine with some of our favorite \\nChick-fil-A items. From our Chick-fil-A family to yours, let\xe2\x80\x99s come together around this delicious recipe from two members of our Field Operations and International teams Priscilla and Caleb Nicholson \xe2\x80\x93 Deluxe \\nWaffle Fries! \\nIngredients: \\n3 Large Chick-fil-A Waffle Fries\\r\\n1 12 count Chick-fil-A Nuggets\\r\\n5 Strips of bacon, cooked and crumbled\\r\\n1 Cup shredded mild cheddar cheese \\n\xc2\xbd Cup White Queso*\\r\\n1 Dollop of sour cream\\r\\n3 Tablespoons diced chives \\n8 oz. Tub Chick-fil-A Ranch Sauce *White Queso:\\r\\n\xc2\xbd Cup whole milk\\r\\n\xc2\xbd lb White American cheese, grated \\nDirections:\\r\\nWash hands for 20 seconds using soap and warm water. For best quality, use chicken immediately after purchase. If not using chicken immediately, pop in the fridge as soon as possible after purchase and remove \\nonce ready for prep.\\r\\n1. Preheat oven to 350F degrees. \\n2. In a saucepan, boil milk and grated American cheese. Wisk until white queso sauce is thick. Set aside.\\r\\n3. On a baking sheet, spread waffle fries evenly as base layer and add layer of nuggets and cheddar cheese. \\nRepeat.\\r\\n4. Nuggets \xe2\x80\x93 a new series from our kitchens to yours. While you\xe2\x80\x99re at home, we thought we\xe2\x80\x99d share some creative ways to change up your dinner routine with some of our favorite \\nChick-fil-A items. From our Chick-fil-A family to yours, let\xe2\x80\x99s come together around this delicious recipe from Owner\\/Operator Britt Sims and her daughter Tatum \xe2\x80\x93 Polynesian Meatloaf! \\nIngredients:\\r\\n1 lb ground turkey (may sub ground chicken) \\n1 lb ground pork (if pork not available, use 2 lb ground turkey\\/chicken+ 1\\/4 C heavy whipping cream) \\n1 medium onion, finely chopped \\n1 medium bell pepper, finely chopped \\n4 garlic cloves, finely chopped \\n2 eggs \\n1\\/3 C Chick-fil-A Polynesian Sauce \\n1 C breadcrumbs \\n1 Tbsp Worcestershire sauce \\n2 Tbsp chopped fresh parsley (or 1 Tbsp dried) \\n1.5 tsp kosher salt \\n\xc2\xbd tsp black pepper \\n\xc2\xbd tsp smoked paprika \\n\xc2\xbc tsp crushed red pepper flakes \\n1\\/3 C Chick-fil-A Polynesian Sauce (topping) \\nDirections:\\r\\nWash hands for 20 seconds using soap and warm water. \\n1. Preheat oven to 375 degrees. \\n2. Prepare a loaf pan \xe2\x80\x93 line with parchment or foil to overlap edges to easily remove meatloaf. \\n3. In a medium mixing bowl, add all ingredients for meatloaf (not topping) & mix together until ingredients are thoroughly combined. \\n4. Press into lined loaf pan and bake in center of oven for 40 minutes. \\n5. After 40 minutes, spread Polynesian sauce to cover meatloaf top. Bake for 12-15 more minutes. Internal temp should be 165 or higher. \\n6. Remove from oven and let cool for 5 minutes in pan. \\n7. Remove from pan carefully and use reserved Polynesian drippings from pan as sauce. \\n8. Delicious served diner-style with mashed potatoes & green peas. Use leftover meatloaf slices to make toasted meatloaf patty melts. From our Chick-fil-A family to yours, let\xe2\x80\x99s come together around this delicious recipe from one member of our Culinary team Shona Jonson and her family \xe2\x80\x93 Spicy Bahn Mi Sandwich!\\n\\nIngredients:\\n\\nPickled Vegetables \\n1\\/2 teaspoon salt \\n1\\/4 cup sugar \\n1\\/4 cup rice vinegar \\n\xc2\xbd cup hot water \\n2 Tablespoons Sweet & Spicy Siracha sauce \\n1 cup cut carrots \\n1 cup cut radish or daikon \\nSweet & Spicy Siracha Mayo \\n1\\/2 cup mayonnaise \\n2 Tablespoons Sweet & Spicy Siracha sauce \\nSandwich \\n4 baguettes or sub rolls \\n4 Chick-fil-A Spicy Filets, sliced into strips \\n1-2 sliced Persian cucumbers \\nFresh cilantro \\nLime slices \\nJalape\xc3\xb1o slices\\n\\nDirections:\\nWash hands for 20 seconds using soap and warm water. For best quality, use chicken immediately after purchase. If not using chicken immediately, pop in the fridge as soon as possible after purchase and remove once ready for prep. \\n1. Place sliced carrots and radish into mason jar or bowl. \\n2. Mix salt, sugar, rice vinegar, hot water and Sweet & Spicy Siracha sauce. Stir until sugar dissolves. \\n3. Pour liquid over veggies, cover and chill in the refrigerator for up to 3 days. \\n4. Mix mayonnaise and Sweet and Spicy Siracha sauce until well blended. Store in the refrigerator for up to 3 days. \\n5. Once vegetables and mayo are ready, prepare sandwich toppings by first toasting baguettes, if desired.\\n6. Spread bread with Sweet & Spicy Siracha Mayo. \\n7. Top with cucumbers, chicken, pickled veggies and cilantro. \\n8. Add lime juice and\\/or jalape\xc3\xb1o, if desired.
